        <article class="post-8550 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-sports tag-2939 tag-fifa tag-world-cup" id="post-8550">
         <a aria-hidden="true" class="post-thumbnail" href="https://bookofthrees.com/fifa-2018-top-3-players/">
          <img alt="FIFA 2018 Top 3 Players" class="attachment-post-thumbnail size-post-thumbnail wp-post-image" height="372" src="https://i0.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/image-2.jpg?resize=672%2C372&amp;ssl=1" width="672"/>
         </a>
         <header class="entry-header">
          <div class="entry-meta">
           <span class="cat-links">
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/category/chapters/sports/" rel="category tag">
             Sports
            </a>
           </span>
          </div>
          <h1 class="entry-title">
           <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/fifa-2018-top-3-players/" rel="bookmark">
            FIFA 2018 Top 3 Players
           </a>
          </h1>
          <div class="entry-meta">
           <span class="entry-date">
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/fifa-2018-top-3-players/" rel="bookmark">
             <time class="entry-date" datetime="2018-06-22T14:13:15+00:00">
              June 22, 2018
             </time>
            </a>
           </span>
           <span class="byline">
            <span class="author vcard">
             <a class="url fn n" href="https://bookofthrees.com/author/threes/" rel="author">
              Threes
             </a>
            </span>
           </span>
          </div>
          <!-- .entry-meta -->
         </header>
         <!-- .entry-header -->
         <div class="entry-content">
          <p>
           <a href="https://i0.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/image.jpg?ssl=1">
            <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-8546" data-recalc-dims="1" height="169" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" src="https://i2.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/image.jpg?resize=300%2C169&amp;ssl=1" srcset="https://i2.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/image.jpg?resize=300%2C169&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/image.jpg?resize=768%2C432&amp;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/image.jpg?w=850&amp;ssl=1 850w" width="300"/>
           </a>
          </p>
          <p>
           PARIS SAINT-GERMAIN
          </p>
          <ol>
           <li>
            NEYMAR
            <br/>
            The most expensive player in the world, Neymar recently headed for Paris in a move that shocked the football world. While still slightly below Messi and Ronaldo, Neymar is in the upper echelons of the talent-packed history of Brazilian football. His 92 Pace makes him one of the fastest players out there, and his 94 Dribbling is reminiscent of Ronaldinho at his peak.
           </li>
          </ol>
          <p>
           <a href="https://i1.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/image-1.jpg?ssl=1">
            <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-8547" data-recalc-dims="1" height="169" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" src="https://i0.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/image-1.jpg?resize=300%2C169&amp;ssl=1" srcset="https://i0.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/image-1.jpg?resize=300%2C169&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/image-1.jpg?resize=768%2C432&amp;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/image-1.jpg?w=850&amp;ssl=1 850w" width="300"/>
           </a>
          </p>
          <p>
           FC BARCELONA
          </p>
          <ol>
           <li>
            LIONEL MESSI
            <br/>
            In a constant battle for best in the world (and of all-time), it’s hard to say anything about Messi without stretching into hyperbole. His 95 Dribbling is the highest, and very few defenders are able to even come close to stopping him when he’s playing his best. Combined with 89 Pace and 90 Shooting, Messi may usually start on the wing but he always finds a way to get in front of goal—where he rarely misses.
           </li>
          </ol>
          <p>
           <a href="https://i1.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/image-2.jpg?ssl=1">
            <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-8548" data-recalc-dims="1" height="169" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" src="https://i2.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/image-2.jpg?resize=300%2C169&amp;ssl=1" srcset="https://i2.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/image-2.jpg?resize=300%2C169&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/image-2.jpg?resize=768%2C432&amp;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/image-2.jpg?w=850&amp;ssl=1 850w" width="300"/>
           </a>
          </p>
          <p>
           REAL MADRID
          </p>
          <ol>
           <li>
            CRISTIANO RONALDO
            <br/>
            There are few things that Ronaldo cannot do on a pitch, and few attacking positions in which he won’t excel. His 93 Shooting is evidenced by the unreal number of goals he’s scored in the past few seasons, and Ronaldo’s 90 Pace and 90 Dribbling make him virtually untouchable when in top form. Sometimes deployed as a forward, Ronaldo can dance into the box and dispatch the ball into the net without skipping a beat. He is probably at his best on the left wing, where he can create chances for teammates, or as he does more often, cut inside and lash the ball past a helpless goalkeeper.
           </li>
          </ol>
          <p>
           Source: EasFifa.com
          </p>
          <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled">

        <article class="post-8545 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-sports tag-fifa tag-hat-trick tag-ronaldo" id="post-8545">
         <header class="entry-header">
          <div class="entry-meta">
           <span class="cat-links">
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/category/chapters/sports/" rel="category tag">
             Sports
            </a>
           </span>
          </div>
          <h1 class="entry-title">
           <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/cristiano-ronaldo-world-cup-2018-hat-trick-goal-portugal-star-makes-history-with-stunning-free-kick-against-spain-the-independent/" rel="bookmark">
            Cristiano Ronaldo World Cup 2018 hat-trick goal: Portugal star makes history with stunning free kick against Spain | The Independent
           </a>
          </h1>
          <div class="entry-meta">
           <span class="entry-date">
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/cristiano-ronaldo-world-cup-2018-hat-trick-goal-portugal-star-makes-history-with-stunning-free-kick-against-spain-the-independent/" rel="bookmark">
             <time class="entry-date" datetime="2018-06-22T13:14:39+00:00">
              June 22, 2018
             </time>
            </a>
           </span>
           <span class="byline">
            <span class="author vcard">
             <a class="url fn n" href="https://bookofthrees.com/author/threes/" rel="author">
              Threes
             </a>
            </span>
           </span>
          </div>
          <!-- .entry-meta -->
         </header>
         <!-- .entry-header -->
         <div class="entry-content">
          <p>
           Cristiano Ronaldo scored a late free-kick to complete a remarkable hat-trick in a thrilling 3-3 draw with Spain on Friday night. The Real Madrid man had scored twice in the first-half of the Group B match, but the reigning European champions looked to be headed to a gruelling defeat thanks to Nacho’s wonder-strike midway through the second-half. However with time running out, Spain conceded a free-kick in a dangerous position when Gerard Pique fouled Ronaldo twenty-five yards out from goal.
           <br/>
           — Read on
           <a href="https://www.independent.co.uk/sport/football/world-cup/cristiano-ronaldo-goal-free-kick-hat-trick-video-watch-portugal-vs-spain-world-cup-2018-a8401436.html">
            www.independent.co.uk/sport/football/world-cup/cristiano-ronaldo-goal-free-kick-hat-trick-video-watch-portugal-vs-spain-world-cup-2018-a8401436.html
           </a>
          </p>

        <article class="post-8506 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-mathematics category-nature category-science tag-buckminster-fuller tag-tetrahedron" id="post-8506">
         <a aria-hidden="true" class="post-thumbnail" href="https://bookofthrees.com/tetrahedron/">
          <img alt="Tetrahedron" class="attachment-post-thumbnail size-post-thumbnail wp-post-image" height="372" sizes="(max-width: 672px) 100vw, 672px" src="https://i2.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/Tetrahedron-puzzle.jpg?resize=672%2C372&amp;ssl=1" srcset="https://i0.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/Tetrahedron-puzzle.jpg?resize=672%2C372&amp;ssl=1 672w, https://i2.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/Tetrahedron-puzzle.jpg?resize=1038%2C576&amp;ssl=1 1038w" width="672"/>
         </a>
         <header class="entry-header">
          <div class="entry-meta">
           <span class="cat-links">
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/category/chapters/mathematics/" rel="category tag">
             Mathematics
            </a>
            ,
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/category/chapters/nature/" rel="category tag">
             Nature
            </a>
            ,
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/category/chapters/science/" rel="category tag">
             Science
            </a>
           </span>
          </div>
          <h1 class="entry-title">
           <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/tetrahedron/" rel="bookmark">
            Tetrahedron
           </a>
          </h1>
          <div class="entry-meta">
           <span class="entry-date">
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/tetrahedron/" rel="bookmark">
             <time class="entry-date" datetime="2018-04-17T10:01:27+00:00">
              April 17, 2018
             </time>
            </a>
           </span>
           <span class="byline">
            <span class="author vcard">
             <a class="url fn n" href="https://bookofthrees.com/author/admin/" rel="author">
              admin
             </a>
            </span>
           </span>
          </div>
          <!-- .entry-meta -->
         </header>
         <!-- .entry-header -->
         <div class="entry-content">
          <figure class="wp-caption alignright" id="attachment_8507" style="width: 240px">
           <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/tetrahedron/240px-tetrahedron-svg/" rel="attachment wp-att-8507">
            <img alt="Tetrahedron" class="size-full wp-image-8507" data-recalc-dims="1" height="227" src="https://i2.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/240px-Tetrahedron.svg_.png?resize=240%2C227&amp;ssl=1" width="240"/>
           </a>
           <figcaption class="wp-caption-text">
            Tetrahedron
           </figcaption>
          </figure>
          <p>
           <span class="Apple-style-span">
            Four triangular faces along with six edges meeting at four vertices together describe the regular tetrahedron.
           </span>
           <span class="Apple-style-span">
            The tetrahedron is the root of all entanglements that shape the perceivable bonds that hold life together in this dimension. The regular tetrahedron can be found at the source of all three-dimensional forms and is fundamental in the creation of all patterns and holographic configurations.
           </span>
          </p>
          <p>
           <span style="font-weight: 400;">
            <em>
             “All of the definable structuring of Universe is tetrahedrally coordinate in rational number increments of the tetrahedron. By tetrahedron, we mean the minimum thinkable set that would subdivide the Universe and have the interconnectedness where it comes back upon itself. The basic structural unit of physical Universe quantation, tetrahedron has the fundamental prime number oneness.”
            </em>
           </span>
          </p>
          <p>
           Buckminster Fuller
          </p>
          <p style="font-weight: 400;">
           <em>
            “Within it (tetrahedron) lies the energy that holds all life together. The bonds that hold atoms, particles and molecules together, all the way down to nanoparticles and all the way up to macroparticles, are tetrahedral. Everything that exists as you conceive of it in a 3-dimensional world, is held together by these tetrahedral bonds.”
           </em>
          </p>
          <p>
           Buckminster Fuller
          </p>
          <p style="font-weight: 400;">
           <em>
            “The tetrahedron is a form of energy package. The tetrahedron is transformable…All of the definable structuring of Universe is tetrahedrally coordinate in rational number increments of the tetrahedron.”
           </em>
          </p>
          <p style="font-weight: 400;">
           Buckminster Fuller
          </p>
          <figure class="wp-caption alignleft" id="attachment_8508" style="width: 300px">
           <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/tetrahedron/620-06-tetrahedron/" rel="attachment wp-att-8508">
            <img alt="2 Triangles forming a Tetrahedron" class="size-medium wp-image-8508" data-recalc-dims="1" height="210" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" src="https://i2.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/620.06-Tetrahedron.png?resize=300%2C210&amp;ssl=1" srcset="https://i0.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/620.06-Tetrahedron.png?resize=300%2C210&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/620.06-Tetrahedron.png?resize=768%2C536&amp;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/620.06-Tetrahedron.png?w=899&amp;ssl=1 899w" width="300"/>
           </a>
           <figcaption class="wp-caption-text">
            2 Triangles forming a Tetrahedron
           </figcaption>
          </figure>
          <p style="font-weight: 400;">
           <em>
            “Two Triangular Energy Events Make Tetrahedron: The open-ended triangular spiral can be considered one “energy event” consisting of an action, reaction and resultant. Two such events (one positive and one negative) combine to form the tetrahedron.”
           </em>
          </p>
          <p style="font-weight: 400;">
           Buckminster Fuller
          </p>
          <p>
          </p>

        <article class="post-8499 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-history-politics category-c80-language tag-hebrew tag-metric" id="post-8499">
         <a aria-hidden="true" class="post-thumbnail" href="https://bookofthrees.com/hebrew-the-metric-system-of-languages/">
          <img alt="Hebrew: The Metric System of Languages" class="attachment-post-thumbnail size-post-thumbnail wp-post-image" height="217" src="https://i2.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/39FC2EF9-208F-4645-AC69-6C44CECA87A7-698-0000009DD3B64A2A.jpeg?resize=220%2C217&amp;ssl=1" width="220"/>
         </a>
         <header class="entry-header">
          <div class="entry-meta">
           <span class="cat-links">
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/category/chapters/history-politics/" rel="category tag">
             History - Politics
            </a>
            ,
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/category/chapters/c80-language/" rel="category tag">
             Language
            </a>
           </span>
          </div>
          <h1 class="entry-title">
           <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/hebrew-the-metric-system-of-languages/" rel="bookmark">
            Hebrew: The Metric System of Languages
           </a>
          </h1>
          <div class="entry-meta">
           <span class="entry-date">
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/hebrew-the-metric-system-of-languages/" rel="bookmark">
             <time class="entry-date" datetime="2018-04-15T22:47:08+00:00">
              April 15, 2018
             </time>
            </a>
           </span>
           <span class="byline">
            <span class="author vcard">
             <a class="url fn n" href="https://bookofthrees.com/author/admin/" rel="author">
              admin
             </a>
            </span>
           </span>
          </div>
          <!-- .entry-meta -->
         </header>
         <!-- .entry-header -->
         <div class="entry-content">
          <p>
           Guest Post by Bob Canter
          </p>
          <p>
           <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/hebrew-the-metric-system-of-languages/98743a57-931f-4b60-bc07-f0b2d3824689-698-0000009b3ebe757c/" rel="attachment wp-att-8502">
            <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-medium wp-image-8502" data-recalc-dims="1" height="200" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" src="https://i0.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/98743A57-931F-4B60-BC07-F0B2D3824689-698-0000009B3EBE757C.jpeg?resize=300%2C200&amp;ssl=1" srcset="https://i1.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/98743A57-931F-4B60-BC07-F0B2D3824689-698-0000009B3EBE757C.jpeg?resize=300%2C200&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/98743A57-931F-4B60-BC07-F0B2D3824689-698-0000009B3EBE757C.jpeg?resize=768%2C512&amp;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/98743A57-931F-4B60-BC07-F0B2D3824689-698-0000009B3EBE757C.jpeg?w=960&amp;ssl=1 960w" width="300"/>
           </a>
          </p>
          <p>
           Created roughly a century apart, the advent of modern Hebrew and the creation of the Metric System bear several striking similarities.
          </p>
          <p style="text-align: left;">
           Hebrew exhibits some of the same logical features as does the Metric System. The primary logical structure of Hebrew is the three-letter root system which forms the building blocks of most Hebrew words. Understanding these many roots is not only a fascinating exercise in linguistic exploration, but is a key step in building a Hebrew vocabulary.
          </p>
          <p>
           For example, the three-letter root samech-fay-resh (ס פ ר) means “to recount,” or “telling,” as in the sense of telling a story. From this root Hebrew derives a delightful group of words:
          </p>
          <p>
           ס פ ר = Book
           <br/>
           ס ו פ ר = Author/writer/scribe
           <br/>
           ס פ ר ו ת = Literature
           <br/>
           ס פ ר י ה = Library
           <br/>
           ס פ ר ן = Librarian
           <br/>
           ס פ ר ו ן= Booklet/pamphlet
           <br/>
           ח נ ו ת ס פ ר י ם = Bookstore
           <br/>
           בּ י ת ס פ ר = School (lit., “House of [the] Book”
           <br/>
           ס פ ו ר = Story
           <br/>
           ל ס פ ר = To tell
          </p>
          <figure class="wp-caption alignright" id="attachment_8503" style="width: 300px">
           <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/hebrew-the-metric-system-of-languages/f91d1224-439a-4e60-be19-ff0e9a6bf560-698-0000009d2cfd684f/" rel="attachment wp-att-8503">
            <img alt="Tetragrammaton " class="size-medium wp-image-8503" data-recalc-dims="1" height="290" src="https://i1.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/F91D1224-439A-4E60-BE19-FF0E9A6BF560-698-0000009D2CFD684F.jpeg?resize=300%2C290&amp;ssl=1" width="300"/>
           </a>
           <figcaption class="wp-caption-text">
            Tetragrammaton
           </figcaption>
          </figure>
          <p>
           And like the Metric System, Hebrew employs a series of prefixes that are attached to the words they modify:
          </p>
          <p>
           ה for “The” “This” or “That”
           <br/>
           ו for “And”/”And the”
           <br/>
           ל for “To/”To the”
           <br/>
           בּ for “In/”In the”/”At”
           <br/>
           מ or מִן for “From”/”From the”
          </p>
          <p>
           The logic of Hebrew is that if you can recognize the root in Hebrew, and learn its meaning, then even when you see a word with that three-letter root that you do not know, you can figure that it must have some logical relationship to the base meaning of that root; in the above case any Hebrew word with the three-letter root samech-fay-resh (ס פ ר) will have some relationship to “recounting” or “telling.”
          </p>
          <p style="text-align: left;">
           Read the full article and learn Hebrew at
           <a href="https://blogs.transparent.com/hebrew/hebrew-the-metric-system-of-languages/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
            https://blogs.transparent.com/hebrew/hebrew-the-metric-system-of-languages/
           </a>
          </p>
          <p>
          </p>
          <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled">

        <article class="post-8432 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-history-politics category-mathematics category-science tag-universe" id="post-8432">
         <a aria-hidden="true" class="post-thumbnail" href="https://bookofthrees.com/the-shape-of-the-universe/">
          <img alt="The shape of the universe" class="attachment-post-thumbnail size-post-thumbnail wp-post-image" height="370" sizes="(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px" src="https://i2.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/shape-of-universe-1.jpg?resize=600%2C370&amp;ssl=1" srcset="https://i0.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/shape-of-universe-1.jpg?w=600&amp;ssl=1 600w, https://i1.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/shape-of-universe-1.jpg?resize=300%2C185&amp;ssl=1 300w" width="600"/>
         </a>
         <header class="entry-header">
          <div class="entry-meta">
           <span class="cat-links">
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/category/chapters/history-politics/" rel="category tag">
             History - Politics
            </a>
            ,
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/category/chapters/mathematics/" rel="category tag">
             Mathematics
            </a>
            ,
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/category/chapters/science/" rel="category tag">
             Science
            </a>
           </span>
          </div>
          <h1 class="entry-title">
           <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/the-shape-of-the-universe/" rel="bookmark">
            The shape of the universe
           </a>
          </h1>
          <div class="entry-meta">
           <span class="entry-date">
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/the-shape-of-the-universe/" rel="bookmark">
             <time class="entry-date" datetime="2018-04-06T13:58:10+00:00">
              April 6, 2018
             </time>
            </a>
           </span>
           <span class="byline">
            <span class="author vcard">
             <a class="url fn n" href="https://bookofthrees.com/author/admin/" rel="author">
              admin
             </a>
            </span>
           </span>
          </div>
          <!-- .entry-meta -->
         </header>
         <!-- .entry-header -->
         <div class="entry-content">
          <figure class="wp-caption aligncenter" id="attachment_8486" style="width: 300px">
           <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/the-shape-of-the-universe/what-shape-is-the-universe/" rel="attachment wp-att-8486">
            <img alt="What shape is the Universe" class="wp-image-8486 size-medium" data-recalc-dims="1" height="217" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" src="https://i2.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/What-shape-is-the-Universe.jpg?resize=300%2C217&amp;ssl=1" srcset="https://i1.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/What-shape-is-the-Universe.jpg?resize=300%2C217&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/What-shape-is-the-Universe.jpg?resize=768%2C554&amp;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/What-shape-is-the-Universe.jpg?resize=1024%2C739&amp;ssl=1 1024w, https://i0.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/What-shape-is-the-Universe.jpg?w=1280&amp;ssl=1 1280w, https://i2.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/What-shape-is-the-Universe.jpg?w=948&amp;ssl=1 948w" width="300"/>
           </a>
           <figcaption class="wp-caption-text">
            What shape is the Universe?
           </figcaption>
          </figure>
          <p>
           There are three possible geometries of the universe: closed, open and flat from top to bottom. The closed universe is of finite size and, due to its curvature, traveling far enough in one direction will lead back to one’s starting point. The open and flat universes are infinite and traveling in a constant direction will never lead to the same point.
          </p>
          <p>
           Universe with positive
           <b>
            curvature
           </b>
           . A positively
           <b>
            curved
           </b>
           universe is described by elliptic geometry, and can be thought of as a three-dimensional hypersphere, or some other
           <b>
            spherical
           </b>
           3-manifold (such as the Poincaré
           <b>
            dodecahedral
           </b>
           space), all of which are quotients of the 3-sphere.
          </p>
          <p>
           <a class="more-link" href="https://bookofthrees.com/the-shape-of-the-universe/#more-8432">
            Continue reading
            <span class="screen-reader-text">
             The shape of the universe
            </span>
            <span class="meta-nav">
             →
            </span>
           </a>
          </p>
          <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled">
           <div class="robots-nocontent sd-block sd-social sd-social-icon-text sd-sharing">

        <article class="post-8471 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-entertainment category-history-politics tag-kate-middleton tag-prince-william tag-royals" id="post-8471">
         <a aria-hidden="true" class="post-thumbnail" href="https://bookofthrees.com/prince-william-and-kate-middletons-third-child-will-not-have-a-last-name/">
          <img alt="Prince William and Kate Middleton’s Third Child Will Not Have a Last Name" class="attachment-post-thumbnail size-post-thumbnail wp-post-image" height="372" src="https://i2.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/Prince-William-and-Kate-Middleton.jpg?resize=672%2C372&amp;ssl=1" width="672"/>
         </a>
         <header class="entry-header">
          <div class="entry-meta">
           <span class="cat-links">
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/category/chapters/entertainment/" rel="category tag">
             Entertainment
            </a>
            ,
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/category/chapters/history-politics/" rel="category tag">
             History - Politics
            </a>
           </span>
          </div>
          <h1 class="entry-title">
           <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/prince-william-and-kate-middletons-third-child-will-not-have-a-last-name/" rel="bookmark">
            Prince William and Kate Middleton’s Third Child Will Not Have a Last Name
           </a>
          </h1>
          <div class="entry-meta">
           <span class="entry-date">
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/prince-william-and-kate-middletons-third-child-will-not-have-a-last-name/" rel="bookmark">
             <time class="entry-date" datetime="2018-04-06T13:33:35+00:00">
              April 6, 2018
             </time>
            </a>
           </span>
           <span class="byline">
            <span class="author vcard">
             <a class="url fn n" href="https://bookofthrees.com/author/admin/" rel="author">
              admin
             </a>
            </span>
           </span>
          </div>
          <!-- .entry-meta -->
         </header>
         <!-- .entry-header -->
         <div class="entry-content">
          <figure class="wp-caption aligncenter" id="attachment_8482" style="width: 300px">
           <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/prince-william-and-kate-middletons-third-child-will-not-have-a-last-name/prince-william-and-kate-middleton-and-children/" rel="attachment wp-att-8482">
            <img alt="Prince William and Kate Middleton and Children" class="size-medium wp-image-8482" data-recalc-dims="1" height="233" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" src="https://i1.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/Prince-William-and-Kate-Middleton-and-Children.jpg?resize=300%2C233&amp;ssl=1" srcset="https://i1.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/Prince-William-and-Kate-Middleton-and-Children.jpg?resize=300%2C233&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/Prince-William-and-Kate-Middleton-and-Children.jpg?w=768&amp;ssl=1 768w" width="300"/>
           </a>
           <figcaption class="wp-caption-text">
            Prince William and Kate Middleton and Children
           </figcaption>
          </figure>
          <p>
           Most families pass down a last name from one generation to the next, but the British royal family follows their own rules and traditions. They have formal titles that are made up of up to 15 words, but tend to only use Prince or Princess in front of their given name.
          </p>
          <p>
           However, with the birth of Prince William and Kate Middleton’s third child taking place any day now, many are curious as to whether he or she will adopt the surname the descendants of Prince Phillip and Queen Elizabeth often use on certain occasions: Mountbatten-Windsor.
          </p>
          <p>
           <a class="more-link" href="https://bookofthrees.com/prince-william-and-kate-middletons-third-child-will-not-have-a-last-name/#more-8471">
            Continue reading
            <span class="screen-reader-text">
             Prince William and Kate Middleton’s Third Child Will Not Have a Last Name
            </span>
            <span class="meta-nav">
             →
            </span>
           </a>
          </p>

        <article class="post-8468 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-business-economics category-science tag-blockchain tag-cryptocurrencies" id="post-8468">
         <a aria-hidden="true" class="post-thumbnail" href="https://bookofthrees.com/cryptocurrencies-explained-how-blockchain-technology-could-solve-3-big-problems-plaguing-the-art-industry/">
          <img alt="Cryptocurrencies, Explained: How Blockchain Technology Could Solve 3 Big Problems Plaguing the Art Industry" class="attachment-post-thumbnail size-post-thumbnail wp-post-image" height="372" src="https://i1.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/Blockchain-Funds.png?resize=672%2C372&amp;ssl=1" width="672"/>
         </a>
         <header class="entry-header">
          <div class="entry-meta">
           <span class="cat-links">
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/category/chapters/business-economics/" rel="category tag">
             Business - Economics
            </a>
            ,
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/category/chapters/science/" rel="category tag">
             Science
            </a>
           </span>
          </div>
          <h1 class="entry-title">
           <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/cryptocurrencies-explained-how-blockchain-technology-could-solve-3-big-problems-plaguing-the-art-industry/" rel="bookmark">
            Cryptocurrencies, Explained: How Blockchain Technology Could Solve 3 Big Problems Plaguing the Art Industry
           </a>
          </h1>
          <div class="entry-meta">
           <span class="entry-date">
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/cryptocurrencies-explained-how-blockchain-technology-could-solve-3-big-problems-plaguing-the-art-industry/" rel="bookmark">
             <time class="entry-date" datetime="2018-03-23T21:12:56+00:00">
              March 23, 2018
             </time>
            </a>
           </span>
           <span class="byline">
            <span class="author vcard">
             <a class="url fn n" href="https://bookofthrees.com/author/admin/" rel="author">
              admin
             </a>
            </span>
           </span>
          </div>
          <!-- .entry-meta -->
         </header>
         <!-- .entry-header -->
         <div class="entry-content">
          <ul>
           <li>
            <strong>
             PROBLEM 1: THE LINGERING MYSTERIES OF PROVENANCE &amp; AUTHENTICITY
            </strong>
           </li>
           <li>
            <strong>
             PROBLEM 2: THE WEIGHT OF THE TRADITIONAL FINANCE SYSTEM
            </strong>
           </li>
           <li>
            <strong>
             PROBLEM 3: THE BURDEN OF TRADITIONAL CONTRACTS
             <br/>
            </strong>
            __________________________________________________________________
           </li>
          </ul>
          <figure class="wp-caption aligncenter" id="attachment_8473" style="width: 474px">
           <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/cryptocurrencies-explained-how-blockchain-technology-could-solve-3-big-problems-plaguing-the-art-industry/blockchain-2/" rel="attachment wp-att-8473">
            <img alt="blockchain" class="size-large wp-image-8473" data-recalc-dims="1" height="284" sizes="(max-width: 474px) 100vw, 474px" src="https://i2.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/blockchain.jpg?resize=474%2C284&amp;ssl=1" srcset="https://i1.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/blockchain.jpg?resize=1024%2C614&amp;ssl=1 1024w, https://i2.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/blockchain.jpg?resize=300%2C180&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/blockchain.jpg?resize=768%2C461&amp;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/blockchain.jpg?w=1500&amp;ssl=1 1500w, https://i1.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/blockchain.jpg?w=948&amp;ssl=1 948w, https://i2.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/blockchain.jpg?w=1422&amp;ssl=1 1422w" width="474"/>
           </a>
           <figcaption class="wp-caption-text">
            blockchain
           </figcaption>
          </figure>
          <h4>
           <strong>
            PROBLEM 1: THE LINGERING MYSTERIES OF PROVENANCE &amp; AUTHENTICITY
           </strong>
          </h4>
          <p>
           Relatively few artworks today offer the air-tight security of a certificate of authenticity backed by an unbroken chain of title. Gaps in the provenance paper trail undermine both sides of the market, with collectors often left to wonder if they’re being presented looted works or outright fakes, and sellers sometimes forced to accept lower offers due to buyers’ hesitance over the uncertainties.
          </p>
          <p>
           <a class="more-link" href="https://bookofthrees.com/cryptocurrencies-explained-how-blockchain-technology-could-solve-3-big-problems-plaguing-the-art-industry/#more-8468">
            Continue reading
            <span class="screen-reader-text">
             Cryptocurrencies, Explained: How Blockchain Technology Could Solve 3 Big Problems Plaguing the Art Industry
            </span>
            <span class="meta-nav">
             →
            </span>
           </a>
          </p>

        <article class="post-8433 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-entertainment tag-bride tag-groom tag-wedding" id="post-8433">
         <a aria-hidden="true" class="post-thumbnail" href="https://bookofthrees.com/the-grooms-guide-to-weddings/">
          <img alt="The grooms guide to Weddings" class="attachment-post-thumbnail size-post-thumbnail wp-post-image" height="333" src="https://i1.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/img_1365.jpg?resize=672%2C333&amp;ssl=1" width="672"/>
         </a>
         <header class="entry-header">
          <div class="entry-meta">
           <span class="cat-links">
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/category/chapters/entertainment/" rel="category tag">
             Entertainment
            </a>
           </span>
          </div>
          <h1 class="entry-title">
           <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/the-grooms-guide-to-weddings/" rel="bookmark">
            The grooms guide to Weddings
           </a>
          </h1>
          <div class="entry-meta">
           <span class="entry-date">
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/the-grooms-guide-to-weddings/" rel="bookmark">
             <time class="entry-date" datetime="2018-03-09T11:37:08+00:00">
              March 9, 2018
             </time>
            </a>
           </span>
           <span class="byline">
            <span class="author vcard">
             <a class="url fn n" href="https://bookofthrees.com/author/admin/" rel="author">
              admin
             </a>
            </span>
           </span>
          </div>
          <!-- .entry-meta -->
         </header>
         <!-- .entry-header -->
         <div class="entry-content">
          <p>
           <img alt="Grooms" class="size-full wp-image-8434" data-recalc-dims="1" height="317" sizes="(max-width: 474px) 100vw, 474px" src="https://i1.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/img_1366.jpg?resize=474%2C317&amp;ssl=1" srcset="https://i2.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/img_1366.jpg?w=768&amp;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/img_1366.jpg?resize=300%2C200&amp;ssl=1 300w" width="474"/>
          </p>
          <p>
           Guys, your wife has been thinking about her big wedding day for some time now. She’s going to have a lot on her plate with planning, picking out color schemes, and all the minor details that are going to bring this special day together.
          </p>
          <p>
           Your role is to help make this job easier for your wife. There are some things you’ll only help out with and other duties that will be yours alone. This is the perfect time to show your support and show that you’re involved.
          </p>
          <p>
           <strong>
            Before the Wedding
           </strong>
          </p>
          <p>
           <img alt="Before the wedding" class="size-full wp-image-8442" data-recalc-dims="1" height="183" src="https://i0.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/img_1367-1.jpg?resize=276%2C183&amp;ssl=1" width="276"/>
           The groom’s duties before the wedding are all about providing support. You want to make sure to show your wife that you’re ready to do this and you’re committed right from the start. This period is about getting yourself in the right state of mind.
          </p>
          <p>
           <a class="more-link" href="https://bookofthrees.com/the-grooms-guide-to-weddings/#more-8433">
            Continue reading
            <span class="screen-reader-text">
             The grooms guide to Weddings
            </span>
            <span class="meta-nav">
             →
            </span>
           </a>
          </p>

           <div class="robots-nocontent sd-block sd-social sd-social-icon-text sd-sharing">

        <article class="post-8423 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-history-politics category-religion tag-ashes-to-ashes tag-dust-to-dust tag-earth-to-earth" id="post-8423">
         <a aria-hidden="true" class="post-thumbnail" href="https://bookofthrees.com/burial-service-earth-to-earth/">
          <img alt="burial service – earth to earth" class="attachment-post-thumbnail size-post-thumbnail wp-post-image" height="372" src="https://i0.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/tomb.jpg?resize=672%2C372&amp;ssl=1" width="672"/>
         </a>
         <header class="entry-header">
          <div class="entry-meta">
           <span class="cat-links">
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/category/chapters/history-politics/" rel="category tag">
             History - Politics
            </a>
            ,
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/category/chapters/religion/" rel="category tag">
             Religion
            </a>
           </span>
          </div>
          <h1 class="entry-title">
           <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/burial-service-earth-to-earth/" rel="bookmark">
            burial service – earth to earth
           </a>
          </h1>
          <div class="entry-meta">
           <span class="entry-date">
            <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/burial-service-earth-to-earth/" rel="bookmark">
             <time class="entry-date" datetime="2018-02-19T14:02:28+00:00">
              February 19, 2018
             </time>
            </a>
           </span>
           <span class="byline">
            <span class="author vcard">
             <a class="url fn n" href="https://bookofthrees.com/author/admin/" rel="author">
              admin
             </a>
            </span>
           </span>
          </div>
          <!-- .entry-meta -->
         </header>
         <!-- .entry-header -->
         <div class="entry-content">
          <p>
           <strong>
            Earth to earth, ashes to ashes, dust to dust.
           </strong>
          </p>
          <figure class="wp-caption alignright" id="attachment_8425" style="width: 300px">
           <a href="https://bookofthrees.com/burial-service-earth-to-earth/ashes-to-ashes/" rel="attachment wp-att-8425">
            <img alt="ashes to ashes" class="size-medium wp-image-8425" data-recalc-dims="1" height="194" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" src="https://i2.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/ashes-to-ashes.jpg?resize=300%2C194&amp;ssl=1" srcset="https://i0.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/ashes-to-ashes.jpg?resize=300%2C194&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/bookofthrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/ashes-to-ashes.jpg?w=330&amp;ssl=1 330w" width="300"/>
           </a>
           <figcaption class="wp-caption-text">
            ashes to ashes
           </figcaption>
          </figure>
          <p>
           Forasmuch as it hath pleased Almighty God of his great mercy to take unto himself the soul of our dear brother here departed, we therefore commit his body to the ground;
           <strong>
            earth to earth
           </strong>
           ,
           <strong>
            ashes to ashes
           </strong>
           ,
           <strong>
            dust to dust
           </strong>
           ; in sure and certain hope of the Resurrection to eternal life, through our Lord Jesus Christ; who shall …
          </p>
          <p>
           Ashes to ashes’ derives from the
           <em>
            English Burial Service
           </em>
           . The text of that service is adapted from the Biblical text,
           <em>
            Genesis 3:19
           </em>
           (
           <a href="https://www.phrases.org.uk/meanings/bible-phrases-sayings.html">
            King James Version
           </a>
           ):
           <a class="more-link" href="https://bookofthrees.com/burial-service-earth-to-earth/#more-8423">
            Continue reading
            <span class="screen-reader-text">
             burial service – earth to earth
            </span>
            <span class="meta-nav">
             →
            </span>
           </a>
          </p>

       function bwg_move_filmstrip_0() {
         var image_left = jQuery(".bwg_slideshow_thumb_active_0").position().left;
         var image_right = jQuery(".bwg_slideshow_thumb_active_0").position().left + jQuery(".bwg_slideshow_thumb_active_0").outerWidth(true);
         var bwg_filmstrip_width = jQuery(".bwg_slideshow_filmstrip_0").outerWidth(true);
         var bwg_filmstrip_thumbnails_width = jQuery(".bwg_slideshow_filmstrip_thumbnails_0").outerWidth(true);
         var long_filmstrip_cont_left = jQuery(".bwg_slideshow_filmstrip_thumbnails_0").position().left;
         var long_filmstrip_cont_right = Math.abs(jQuery(".bwg_slideshow_filmstrip_thumbnails_0").position().left) + bwg_filmstrip_width;
         if (bwg_filmstrip_width > bwg_filmstrip_thumbnails_width) {
           return;
         }
         if (image_left < Math.abs(long_filmstrip_cont_left)) {
           jQuery(".bwg_slideshow_filmstrip_thumbnails_0").animate({
             left: -image_left
           }, {
             duration: 500,

           });
         }
         else if (image_right > long_filmstrip_cont_right) {
           jQuery(".bwg_slideshow_filmstrip_thumbnails_0").animate({

       function bwg_testDom_0(prop) {
         /* Browser vendor CSS prefixes.*/
         var browserVendors = ['', '-webkit-', '-moz-', '-ms-', '-o-', '-khtml-'];
         /* Browser vendor DOM prefixes.*/
         var domPrefixes = ['', 'Webkit', 'Moz', 'ms', 'O', 'Khtml'];
         var i = domPrefixes.length;
         while (i--) {
           if (typeof document.body.style[domPrefixes[i] + prop] !== 'undefined') {
             return true;
           }
         }
         return false;
       }

           jQuery(next_image_class).fadeTo(bwg_transition_duration_0, 1);
         }
       }
